    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Audio], [e].[CreatedDate], [e].[Description], [e].[Image], [e].[PodcastId], [e].[Title], [l].[Id] AS [Id0], [l].[AppUserId], [l].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [l].[EpisodeId], [t1].[Id] AS [Id1], [t1].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate1], [t1].[EpisodeId] AS [EpisodeId0], [t1].[GuestId], [t1].[Id0] AS [Id00], [t1].[CreatedDate0] AS [CreatedDate00], [t1].[Email], [t1].[FirstName], [t1].[Image] AS [Image0], [t1].[Information], [t1].[LastName], [t1].[SocialMedia]
    FROM [Episodes] AS [e]
    LEFT JOIN [Likes] AS [l] ON [e].[Id] = [l].[EpisodeId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [e0].[Id], [e0].[CreatedDate], [e0].[EpisodeId], [e0].[GuestId], [g].[Id] AS [Id0], [g].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [g].[Email], [g].[FirstName], [g].[Image], [g].[Information], [g].[LastName], [g].[SocialMedia]
        FROM [EpisodeGuests] AS [e0]
        INNER JOIN [Guests] AS [g] ON [e0].[GuestId] = [g].[Id]
    ) AS [t1] ON [e].[Id] = [t1].[EpisodeId]
) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[PodcastId]
ORDER BY [p].[CreatedDate] DESC, [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[Id1]
